<script type='text/javascript'>
//<![CDATA[

function removeHtmlTag(strx,chop){ 
	if(strx.indexOf("<")!=-1)
	{
		var s = strx.split("<"); 
		for(var i=0;i<s.length;i++){ 
			if(s[i].indexOf(">")!=-1){ 
				s[i] = s[i].substring(s[i].indexOf(">")+1,s[i].length); 
			} 
		} 
		strx =  s.join(""); 
	}
	chop = (chop < strx.length-1) ? chop : strx.length-2; 
	while(strx.charAt(chop-1)!=' ' && strx.indexOf(' ',chop)!=-1) chop++; 
	strx = strx.substring(0,chop-1); 
	return strx+'...'; 
}

function createSummaryAndThumb(pID){
	var div = document.getElementById(pID);
	var imgtag = "";
	var img = div.getElementsByTagName("img");
	var summ = summary_noimg;
	if(img.length>=1) {	
		imgtag = '<img src="'+img[0].src+'" class="pbtthumbimg"/>';
		summ = summary_img;
	}
	
	var summary = imgtag + '<div>' + removeHtmlTag(div.innerHTML,summ) + '</div>';
	div.innerHTML = summary;
}

//]]>
</script>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, 18 February 2016</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>

<header class='entry-header entry-header-index'>
<h2 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='http://www.vibexclusive.com/2016/02/premiere-ruby-gyang-shakara-ft.html'>PREMIERE: Ruby Gyang &#8211; &#8220;Shakara&#8221; ft. Ajebutter 22</a>
</h2>
<div class='entry-meta'>
<span class='posted-on'>2/18/2016 08:19:00 pm</span><span class='byline'>&nbsp;&#8211;&nbsp;by <a href='https://plus.google.com/109171130528120025944' rel='author' title='author profile'>Adesoye Richard</a></span>
<span class='comments-link'><a href='http://www.vibexclusive.com/2016/02/premiere-ruby-gyang-shakara-ft.html#comment-form' onclick=''>0</a>
<span class='dashiconsnbt dashiconsnbt-admin-comments'></span></span>
</div>
</header>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
<div class='post-body entry-content'>
<div id='summary3022871956376652494'><p dir="ltr">Chocolate City Music presents a brand new single from the Soul RnB QueenRuby Gyang titled Shakara. Off the much anticipated &#8216;This is Love&#8217; EP set for release soon, &#8216;Shakara&#8217; features the super talented Ajebutter 22 who definitely brings extra spice to the already groovy tune.</p>
<p dir="ltr">Produced by Jude Abaga, Chopstix and Reinhard and mixed&#160;by Suka Sounds,&#160;&#8216;This is Love&#8217; EP is poised to set up Ruby Gyang as one of Africa&#8217;s finest Soul RnB artist. With her undeniable talent and strength, Ruby shows that African women are taking over&#160;the Industry.</p>
<p dir="ltr">Listen download and enjoy Ruby Gyang&#8217;s &#8216;Shakara&#8217; featuring Ajebutter 22 as you anticipate &#8216;This is Love&#8217; EP.</p>
<p dir="ltr">&#160;</p>
<p dir="ltr"><b><a href="http://net.tooxclusive.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Ruby-Shakara.mp3">DOWNLOAD&#160;Ruby Gyang &#8211; &#8220;Shakara&#8221; ft. Ajebutter 22</a></b></p>
</div>

<div id='summary3113366967007683931'><p dir="ltr">Five Star General, KCEE is the standard, international Bureau De Changer.&#160;</p>
<p dir="ltr">On the heels of the hugely successful collaborative single &#8216;Ebeano,&#8217; The serial Five Star hitmaker releases his first song for 2016. The Dr. Amir &#8211; produced &#8216;Bureau De Changer&#8217; brings the trademark groove in a hybrid sound where Pop, percussion meets heavy highlife-sque trumpeting.<br>

The limpopo king gets a new name, Enter the life with the new Alhaji Naira!</p>

<div class='post-body entry-content'>
<div id='summary5056231631296886792'><p dir="ltr">Fast rising gospel rapper, Oluwatomi, also known as &#8216;SU the Rapman&#8217;, his here with another single titled &#8216;Olorun WA&#8217;, produced by Limoblaze.</p>
<p dir="ltr">According to Oluwatomi, &#8220;Olorun Wa is a song that explains a bit of what I face as a CHH soldier but above all, I knew that there is GOD (Olorun WA).&#8221;</p>
